***getogen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:getogen.html>getogen</a> (16682)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Past participle of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">tijgen</i>. It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> virtually only used in the sense of <i>raised</i> or <i><a href = vnd.unilang:brought.html>brought</a> up</i>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span>, when the verb <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:tien.html>tien</a></i> (ancestor of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">tijgen</i>) <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> not yet <a href = vnd.unilang:lost.html>lost</a> its meaning of <i>to raise</i> or <i>nurture</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:getogen.html>getogen</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:brought.html>brought</a> up, grown up, raised</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">getugen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*gitiugon</i>. </p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to testify, bear witness, give testimony, especially in court

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to prove, make apparent</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">getugenisse</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">getugen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to bear witness</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">-nisse</i> (modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:getuigen.html>getuigen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-nis</i>). ***geven.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:geven.html>geven</a> (242)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gēven</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">gevan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gebaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geven.html>geven</a></strong>
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:gevoelen.html>gevoelen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*gefuolen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gafōlijaną</i>. </p>
